ph z

Essential: elaa2lem.a


|- ( ph -> A e. AA )

Essential: elaa2lem.an0


|- ( ph -> A =/= 0 )

Essential: elaa2lem.g


|- ( ph -> G e. ( Poly ` ZZ ) )

Essential: elaa2lem.gn0


|- ( ph -> G =/= 0p )

Essential: elaa2lem.ga


|- ( ph -> ( G ` A ) = 0 )

Essential: elaa2lem.m


|- M = inf ( { n e. NN0 | ( ( coeff ` G ) ` n ) =/= 0 } , RR , < )

Essential: elaa2lem.i


|- I = ( k e. NN0 |-> ( ( coeff ` G ) ` ( k + M ) ) )

Essential: elaa2lem.f


|- F = ( z e. CC |-> sum_ k e. ( 0 ... ( ( deg ` G ) - M ) ) ( ( I ` k ) x. ( z ^ k ) ) )

Essential: etransclem33.s

Essential: etransclem33.x


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: etransclem33.p


|- ( ph -> P e. NN )

Essential: etransclem33.m


|- ( ph -> M e. NN0 )

Essential: etransclem33.f


|- F = ( x e. X |-> ( ( x ^ ( P - 1 ) ) x. prod_ j e. ( 1 ... M ) ( ( x - j ) ^ P ) ) )

Essential: etransclem33.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

F is smooth. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Essential: etransclem34.a


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: etransclem34.p


|- ( ph -> P e. NN )

Essential: etransclem34.m


|- ( ph -> M e. NN0 )

Essential: etransclem34.f


|- F = ( x e. X |-> ( ( x ^ ( P - 1 ) ) x. prod_ k e. ( 1 ... M ) ( ( x - k ) ^ P ) ) )

Essential: etransclem34.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

Essential: etransclem34.h


|- H = ( k e. ( 0 ... M ) |-> ( x e. X |-> ( ( x - k ) ^ if ( k = 0 , ( P - 1 ) , P ) ) ) )

Essential: etransclem34.c


|- C = ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m ( 0 ... M ) ) | sum_ k e. ( 0 ... M ) ( c ` k ) = n } )

The N -th derivative of F is continuous. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Essential: etransclem35.p


|- ( ph -> P e. NN )

Essential: etransclem35.m


|- ( ph -> M e. NN0 )

Essential: etransclem35.f


|- F = ( x e. RR |-> ( ( x ^ ( P - 1 ) ) x. prod_ j e. ( 1 ... M ) ( ( x - j ) ^ P ) ) )

Essential: etransclem35.c


|- C = ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m ( 0 ... M ) ) | sum_ j e. ( 0 ... M ) ( c ` j ) = n } )

Essential: etransclem35.d


|- D = ( j e. ( 0 ... M ) |-> if ( j = 0 , ( P - 1 ) , 0 ) )

P does not divide the P-1 -th derivative of F applied to 0 . This is case 2 of the proof in [Juillerat] p. 13 . (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Essential: etransclem47.q


|- ( ph -> Q e. ( ( Poly ` ZZ ) \ { 0p } ) )

Essential: etransclem47.qe0


|- ( ph -> ( Q ` _e ) = 0 )

Essential: etransclem47.a


|- A = ( coeff ` Q )

Essential: etransclem47.a0


|- ( ph -> ( A ` 0 ) =/= 0 )

Essential: etransclem47.m


|- M = ( deg ` Q )

Essential: etransclem47.p


|- ( ph -> P e. Prime )

Essential: etransclem47.ap


|- ( ph -> ( abs ` ( A ` 0 ) ) < P )

Essential: etransclem47.mp


|- ( ph -> ( ! ` M ) < P )

Essential: etransclem47.9


|- ( ph -> ( sum_ j e. ( 0 ... M ) ( ( abs ` ( ( A ` j ) x. ( _e ^c j ) ) ) x. ( M x. ( M ^ ( M + 1 ) ) ) ) x. ( ( ( M ^ ( M + 1 ) ) ^ ( P - 1 ) ) / ( ! ` ( P - 1 ) ) ) ) < 1 )

Essential: etransclem47.f


|- F = ( x e. RR |-> ( ( x ^ ( P - 1 ) ) x. prod_ j e. ( 1 ... M ) ( ( x - j ) ^ P ) ) )

Essential: etransclem47.l


|- L = sum_ j e. ( 0 ... M ) ( ( ( A ` j ) x. ( _e ^c j ) ) x. S. ( 0 (,) j ) ( ( _e ^c -u x ) x. ( F ` x ) ) _d x )

Essential: etransclem47.k


|- K = ( L / ( ! ` ( P - 1 ) ) )

_e is transcendental. Section *5 of [Juillerat] p. 11 can be used as a reference for this proof. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: etransclem47


|- ( ph -> E. k e. ZZ ( k =/= 0 /\ ( abs ` k ) < 1 ) )

Essential: etransclem48.q

Essential: etransclem48.qe0


|- ( ph -> ( Q ` _e ) = 0 )

Essential: etransclem48.a


|- A = ( coeff ` Q )

Essential: etransclem48.a0


|- ( ph -> ( A ` 0 ) =/= 0 )

Essential: etransclem48.m

Essential: etransclem48.c


|- C = sum_ j e. ( 0 ... M ) ( ( abs ` ( ( A ` j ) x. ( _e ^c j ) ) ) x. ( M x. ( M ^ ( M + 1 ) ) ) )

Essential: etransclem48.s


|- S = ( n e. NN0 |-> ( C x. ( ( ( M ^ ( M + 1 ) ) ^ n ) / ( ! ` n ) ) ) )

Essential: etransclem48.i


|- I = inf ( { i e. NN0 | A. n e. ( ZZ>= ` i ) ( abs ` ( S ` n ) ) < 1 } , RR , < )

Essential: etransclem48.t


|- T = sup ( { ( abs ` ( A ` 0 ) ) , ( ! ` M ) , I } , RR* , < )

_e is transcendental. Section *5 of [Juillerat] p. 11 can be used as a reference for this proof. In this lemma, a large enough prime p is chosen: it will be used by subsequent lemmas. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.) (Revised by AV, 28-Sep-2020.)
